 ) If you are always in tension about office work, then try these 10 methods which will make your work very light
 1
 Be the first to list all your work
 iske baad jo kaam sabase zyada jaruri he uski list taiyaar karen
 When you work according to the need, then your work gets done easily
 2
 Email, the work that you spend the most time managing
 isliye kaam ke dauraan thodaa samay nikaalte hue mail ke jawaab dene ke saath-saath gairajaruri mail ko delit karnaa kabhi nahin bhoolen
 3
 kabhi bhi kaam khatm karne ke chakkar main over planning nahin karen
 Carry out only one job at a time
 lagaataar meeting karte rahane se acha he, pehali meeting main jo tay kiya gaya he us par amal karen
 4
 shortkat apnaanaa offis kaam ke dauraan aapke samay ko bachaane main madadgaar ho saktaa he
 For example, keep automatic response massets on mobile
 aisa karne se aapkaa samay bhi bachataa he or aapako phone karne vaale ko samay rahete aapkaa jawaab bhi mil jaataa he
 5
 kaam ke dauraan sabhi kaam ke liye haa kahana jaruri nahin he
 So it is important that you also learn to say 'no'
 kaam hameshaa apni kshamta ke aadhaar par hi chune
 By doing this, the work is completed on time, as well as the faction in it
 6
 In the office, most meetings are held without any agenda
 isliye sabhi meeting atend karne se pehle ye jarur jaan len ki meeting kis mudde par he
 7
 kaam karte-karte kabhi bhi soshal hona nahin bhoolen
 People working around you have a lot of influence on how you behave
 aksar tej aawaaj or rob jamaane vaale logon ko offis main napsand kiya jaataa he
 8
 stress lekar kisi kaam ko nahin karen
 Stress always makes it difficult rather than making your work easier
 9
 Keep everything on your computer, laptop in an organic way
 isse aapako hi kaam main aasaani hogi ar aapkaa samay bhi bachegaa
 10
 sabase aakhri or jaruri baat ki kaam ke dauraan kabhi aalsee nahin hon
 Even a little carelessness towards work can outweigh you
